(.venv) cakidd@cakidd-Legion-5-16IRX9:/opt/msjarvis-rebuild$ # Get the real byte size of what we're talking about
docker exec jarvis-local-resources-db \
  psql -U postgres -d local_resources -P pager=off -c "
SELECT 
  'gis.gbim_entities' AS source,
  COUNT(*) AS rows,
  pg_size_pretty(COUNT(*) * 512) AS est_vector_storage
FROM gis.gbim_entities
UNION ALL
SELECT 
  'gis.geospatial_features',
  COUNT(*),
  pg_size_pretty(COUNT(*) * 512)
FROM gis.geospatial_features;
"
         source          |   rows   | est_vector_storage 
-------------------------+----------+--------------------
 gis.gbim_entities       |  5416521 | 2645 MB
 gis.geospatial_features | 26923473 | 13 GB
(2 rows)

(.venv) cakidd@cakidd-Legion-5-16IRX9:/opt/msjarvis-rebuild$ # What's actually in gbim_entities
docker exec jarvis-local-resources-db \
  psql -U postgres -d local_resources -P pager=off -c "
SELECT column_name, data_type 
FROM information_schema.columns 
WHERE table_schema='gis' AND table_name='gbim_entities'
ORDER BY ordinal_position;
"

# What's in geospatial_features
docker exec jarvis-local-resources-db \
  psql -U postgres -d local_resources -P pager=off -c "
SELECT column_name, data_type 
FROM information_schema.columns 
WHERE table_schema='gis' AND table_name='geospatial_features'
ORDER BY ordinal_position;
"

# Sample 3 rows from each to see real data shape
docker exec jarvis-local-resources-db \
  psql -U postgres -d local_resources -P pager=off -c "
SELECT * FROM gis.gbim_entities LIMIT 3;
"
"ELECT * FROM gis.geospatial_features LIMIT 3;=off -c "
